    <script nomodule="" src="https://assets.zephr.com/zephr-browser/1.5.1/zephr-browser.umd.js"></script>
    
    <script type="module">
      import * as zephrBrowser from 'https://assets.zephr.com/zephr-browser/1.5.1/zephr-browser.modern.js';
    
      // function to get the cookie content
      const getCookieContent = (cookie) => {
        const cookieContent = document.cookie.split(';').find(item => item.trim().startsWith(`${cookie}=`));
        if (!cookieContent) {
          return false;
        }
        const cookieValue = cookieContent.split(`${cookie}=`);
        if (!cookieValue[1]) {
          return false;
        }
        return cookieValue[1];
      };
    
      // on DOMContentLoaded
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', (event) => {
        // set the default payload for Zephr
        const payload = {
          customData : {
            "wallet-connected": false,
          }
        };
    
        // set the JWT token if present
        const identityToken = getCookieContent('TASLogin');
        if (identityToken) {
          payload.jwt = identityToken;
        }
    
        // set the status of wallet connect to true if the cooke is present
        if (getCookieContent('wallet_sub')) {
          payload.customData['wallet-connected'] = true;
        }
    
        // set the meter height
        const meterValue = getCookieContent('time_meter_v2');
        if (meterValue && meterValue.split('|')[0]) {
          payload.customData['meter-height'] = parseInt(meterValue.split('|')[0]);
        }
    
        // get the tags
        const articleTags = "augmented reality,Space,science,false";
    
        // iterate through the tags and add it to the payload as key value
        if (articleTags) {
          const articleTagArray = articleTags.split(',');
          articleTagArray.forEach((element) => {
            payload.customData[`article-tag-${element}`] = true;
          });
        }
    
        zephrBrowser.run(payload)
        .catch(error => {
          console.error(error);
        });
      });
    
      document.addEventListener('zephr.browserDecisionsFinished', (event) => {
        window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
        const { trials, testGroups } = window.Zephr?.accessDetails;
        // A user can be in multiple trials at a given time
        if (trials) {
          for (const trialKey in trials) {
            const trial = trials[trialKey];
            const { usedInDecision } = trial;
            if (usedInDecision) {
              const {
                totalCredits,
                remainingCredits,
                tracker
              } = trial
              const createZephrTrialEvent = (tracker, credits, totalCredits = true) => {
                const label = `${totalCredits ? 'Total' : 'Remaining'} credits: ${credits}`;
                return {
                  event: 'zephr-trial',
                  category: 'zephr-trial',
                  action: tracker,
                  label,
                }
              }
              window.dataLayer.push(createZephrTrialEvent(tracker, totalCredits, true))
              window.dataLayer.push(createZephrTrialEvent(tracker, remainingCredits, false))
            }
          }
        }
    
        // A user can be in multiple test groups
        if (testGroups) {
          for (const key in testGroups) {
            window.dataLayer.push({
              event: 'user_behavior',
              category: 'zephr-test-group',
              action: key,
              label: Zephr.accessDetails.testGroups[key]
            })
          }
        }
    
        const zephrButtons = Array.from(document.getElementsByClassName('zephr-button'));
        zephrButtons.forEach(button => {
          button.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            const { dataset: { eventAction, eventLabel, location }, innerText = '' } = e.currentTarget;
            // Collecting data attrs from the components and pushing to the dataLayer
            window.dataLayer.push({
              event: 'user_behavior',
              category: 'user_behavior',
              action: eventAction,
              label: eventLabel ? eventLabel : e.currentTarget.innerText,
            })
            // If it is a subscribe button, we redirect to the landing page
            if (location) window.location = location;
          })
        })
    })
    </script>

            </div>            <p><span role="presentation" class="dropcap">T</span>he TIME Immersive app brings TIME stories to life before your eyes using the power of augmented reality (AR) and virtual reality (VR). From <a href="http://www.time.com/apollo11">exploring the surface of the moon</a> to the depths of the<a href="http://www.time.com/amazon-ar"> Amazon rain forest</a>, TIME Immersive extends TIME journalism into your living room, classroom or beyond with groundbreaking interactive visual storytelling. Download the app now, and experience TIME in a whole new way. (Available for <a href="https://apps.apple.com/us/app/time-immersive/id1457280646?mt=8" target="_blank" rel="noopener">iOS</a> and <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.time.timeimmersive&amp;e=-EnableAppDetailsPageRedesign" target="_blank">Android</a> devices.)</p>            <h2>What is Augmented Reality?</h2>            <p>Augmented Reality (AR) uses an app on a device like a mobile phone or tablet to layer images, text or sound over the real world, sometimes in an interactive way. Using AR, TIME Immersive can bring objects from the news and history (like the <a href="https://time.com/longform/apollo-11-moon-landing-immersive-experience/">Apollo 11 Lunar Module</a>) into your home, office or classroom, allowing you to view and interact with them in a powerful new way.</p>            <div id="native-ad-inline-1" class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper native-ad " role="complementary" aria-hidden="true">
              
            </div>            <h2>What is Virtual Reality?</h2>            <p>Virtual Reality (VR) is a computer-generated simulation or 360 video that can be viewed in a headset (sometimes called a head-mounted display). Using VR, TIME Immersive will give you a deeper look and first-person perspective on the news, history, and stories shaping our world today.</p>            <p>&nbsp;</p>            <div id="inline-ad-1" class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper " role="complementary" aria-hidden="true">
              
            <div id="google_ads_iframe_21801468956/time//inline1_0__container__" style="border: 0pt none; display: inline-block;"></div></div>            <h2>TIME Immersive Stories:</h2>            <p><a href="http://www.time.com/amazon-ar"> Inside the Amazon: The Dying Forest</a></p>            <p><a href="https://time.com/longform/apollo-11-moon-landing-immersive-experience/">Landing on the Moon</a></p>            <p>&nbsp;</p>            <p><strong>Contact us</strong> at <a href="mailto:TIMEImmersive@time.com?subject=(READER%20FEEDBACK)%20TIME%20Immersive%20App" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer">TIMEImmersive@time.com</a>.</p>            <div class="component inline-article-recirc">

These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.</p></div></div><div class="ot-accordion-layout ot-cat-item ot-vs-config" data-optanongroupid="C0002"><button ot-accordion="true" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ot-desc-id-C0002" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-C0002"></button><!-- Accordion header --><div class="ot-acc-hdr"><div class="ot-plus-minus"><span></span><span></span></div><h4 class="ot-cat-header" id="ot-header-id-C0002">Performance Cookies</h4><div class="ot-tgl"><input type="checkbox" name="ot-group-id-C0002" id="ot-group-id-C0002" aria-checked="true" role="switch" class="category-switch-handler" data-optanongroupid="C0002" checked="" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-C0002"> <label class="ot-switch" for="ot-group-id-C0002"><span class="ot-switch-nob" aria-checked="false" role="switch"></span> <span class="ot-label-txt">Performance Cookies</span></label> </div></div><!-- accordion detail --><div class="ot-acc-grpcntr ot-acc-txt"><p class="ot-acc-grpdesc ot-category-desc" id="ot-desc-id-C0002">These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. &nbsp; &nbsp;All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.</p></div></div><div class="ot-accordion-layout ot-cat-item ot-vs-config" data-optanongroupid="C0005"><button ot-accordion="true" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ot-desc-id-C0005" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-C0005"></button><!-- Accordion header --><div class="ot-acc-hdr"><div class="ot-plus-minus"><span></span><span></span></div><h4 class="ot-cat-header" id="ot-header-id-C0005">Social Media Cookies</h4><div class="ot-tgl"><input type="checkbox" name="ot-group-id-C0005" id="ot-group-id-C0005" aria-checked="true" role="switch" class="category-switch-handler" data-optanongroupid="C0005" checked="" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-C0005"> <label class="ot-switch" for="ot-group-id-C0005"><span class="ot-switch-nob" aria-checked="false" role="switch"></span> <span class="ot-label-txt">Social Media Cookies</span></label> </div></div><!-- accordion detail --><div class="ot-acc-grpcntr ot-acc-txt"><p class="ot-acc-grpdesc ot-category-desc" id="ot-desc-id-C0005">These cookies are set by a range of social media services that we have added to the site to enable you to share our content with your friends and networks. They are capable of tracking your browser across other sites and building up a profile of your interests. This may impact the content and messages you see on other websites you visit. &nbsp; &nbsp;If you do not allow these cookies you may not be able to use or see these sharing tools.</p></div></div><div class="ot-accordion-layout ot-cat-item ot-vs-config" data-optanongroupid="C0004"><button ot-accordion="true" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ot-desc-id-C0004" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-C0004"></button><!-- Accordion header --><div class="ot-acc-hdr"><div class="ot-plus-minus"><span></span><span></span></div><h4 class="ot-cat-header" id="ot-header-id-C0004">Targeting Cookies</h4><div class="ot-tgl"><input type="checkbox" name="ot-group-id-C0004" id="ot-group-id-C0004" aria-checked="true" role="switch" class="category-switch-handler" data-optanongroupid="C0004" checked="" aria-labelledby="ot-header-id-C0004"> <label class="ot-switch" for="ot-group-id-C0004"><span class="ot-switch-nob" aria-checked="false" role="switch"></span> <span class="ot-label-txt">Targeting Cookies</span></label> </div></div><!-- accordion detail --><div class="ot-acc-grpcntr ot-acc-txt"><p class="ot-acc-grpdesc ot-category-desc" id="ot-desc-id-C0004">Targeting cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners.
